  460 code,comment,ctype,linecomment,string :: Int
  461 code = 1
  462 comment = 2
  463 ctype = 3
  464 linecomment = 4
  465 string = 5
  466 alex_action_0 = startComment
  467 alex_action_1 = endComment
  468 alex_action_2 = addToComment
  469 alex_action_3 = addToComment

  474 alex_action_8 = endLineComment

  476 alex_action_10 = endString

  480 alex_action_16 = plain          TOp
  481 alex_action_17 = plain          TVar
  482 alex_action_18 = startCode
  483 alex_action_19 = startCType

  485 alex_action_21 = addon readBin  TNum
  486 alex_action_22 = addon read'    TNum
  487 alex_action_23 = addon read'    TNum
  488 alex_action_24 = plain          TUnknown
  489 alex_action_25 = addToCode
  490 alex_action_26 = addToCode
  491 alex_action_27 = addToCode
  492 alex_action_28 = endCode
  493 alex_action_29 = addToCType
  494 alex_action_30 = addToCType
  495 alex_action_31 = addToCType
  496 alex_action_32 = endCType

  504 -- it for any purpose whatsoever.

  506 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  507 -- INTERNALS and main scanner engine
  508 
  509 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  510 #  define ILIT(n) n#
  511 #  define IBOX(n) (I# (n))
  512 #  define FAST_INT Int#
  513 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  514 #  if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
  515 #    define GTE(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n >=# m))
  516 #    define EQ(n,m) (GHC.Exts.tagToEnum# (n ==# m))
  517 #  else
  518 #    define GTE(n,m) (n >=# m)
  519 #    define EQ(n,m) (n ==# m)
  520 #  endif
  521 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n +# m)
  522 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n -# m)
  523 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n *# m)
  524 #  define NEGATE(n) (negateInt# (n))
  525 #  define IF_GHC(x) (x)
  526 #else
  527 #  define ILIT(n) (n)
  528 #  define IBOX(n) (n)
  529 #  define FAST_INT Int
  530 #  define GTE(n,m) (n >= m)
  531 #  define EQ(n,m) (n == m)
  532 #  define PLUS(n,m) (n + m)
  533 #  define MINUS(n,m) (n - m)
  534 #  define TIMES(n,m) (n * m)
  535 #  define NEGATE(n) (negate (n))
  536 #  define IF_GHC(x)
  537 #endif
  538 
  539 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  540 data AlexAddr = AlexA# Addr#
  541 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
  542 
  543 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt16OffAddr #-}
  544 alexIndexInt16OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  545 alexIndexInt16OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  546 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  547   narrow16Int# i
  548   where
  549         i    = word2Int# ((high `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` low)
  550         high = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  551         low  = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  552         off' = off *# 2#
  553 #else
  554 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  555   GHC.Exts.int16ToInt#
  556 #endif
  557     (indexInt16OffAddr# arr off)
  558 #endif
  559 #else
  560 alexIndexInt16OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  561 #endif
  562 
  563 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  564 {-# INLINE alexIndexInt32OffAddr #-}
  565 alexIndexInt32OffAddr :: AlexAddr -> Int# -> Int#
  566 alexIndexInt32OffAddr (AlexA# arr) off =
  567 #ifdef WORDS_BIGENDIAN
  568   narrow32Int# i
  569   where
  570    i    = word2Int# ((b3 `uncheckedShiftL#` 24#) `or#`
  571                      (b2 `uncheckedShiftL#` 16#) `or#`
  572                      (b1 `uncheckedShiftL#` 8#) `or#` b0)
  573    b3   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 3#)))
  574    b2   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 2#)))
  575    b1   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' +# 1#)))
  576    b0   = int2Word# (ord# (indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
  577    off' = off *# 4#
  578 #else
  579 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ >= 901
  580   GHC.Exts.int32ToInt#
  581 #endif
  582     (indexInt32OffAddr# arr off)
  583 #endif
  584 #else
  585 alexIndexInt32OffAddr = (Data.Array.!)
  586 #endif
  587 
  588 #ifdef ALEX_GHC
  589 -- GHC >= 503, unsafeAt is available from Data.Array.Base.
  590 quickIndex = unsafeAt
  591 #else
  592 quickIndex = (Data.Array.!)
  593 #endif
  594 
  595 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  596 -- Main lexing routines
  597 
  598 data AlexReturn a
  599   = AlexEOF
  600   | AlexError  !AlexInput
  601   | AlexSkip   !AlexInput !Int
  602   | AlexToken  !AlexInput !Int a
  603 
  604 -- alexScan :: AlexInput -> StartCode -> AlexReturn a
  605 alexScan input__ IBOX(sc)
  606   = alexScanUser undefined input__ IBOX(sc)
  607 
  608 alexScanUser user__ input__ IBOX(sc)
  609   = case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  610   (AlexNone, input__') ->
  611     case alexGetByte input__ of
  612       Nothing ->
  613 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  614                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("End of input.") $
  615 #endif
  616                                    AlexEOF
  617       Just _ ->
  618 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  619                                    Debug.Trace.trace ("Error.") $
  620 #endif
  621                                    AlexError input__'
  622 
  623   (AlexLastSkip input__'' len, _) ->
  624 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  625     Debug.Trace.trace ("Skipping.") $
  626 #endif
  627     AlexSkip input__'' len
  628 
  629   (AlexLastAcc k input__''' len, _) ->
  630 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  631     Debug.Trace.trace ("Accept.") $
  632 #endif
  633     AlexToken input__''' len ((Data.Array.!) alex_actions k)
  634 
  635 
  636 -- Push the input through the DFA, remembering the most recent accepting
  637 -- state it encountered.
  638 
  639 alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input len input__ s last_acc =
  640   input__ `seq` -- strict in the input
  641   let
  642   new_acc = (check_accs (alex_accept `quickIndex` IBOX(s)))
  643   in
  644   new_acc `seq`
  645   case alexGetByte input__ of
  646      Nothing -> (new_acc, input__)
  647      Just (c, new_input) ->
  648 #ifdef ALEX_DEBUG
  649       Debug.Trace.trace ("State: " ++ show IBOX(s) ++ ", char: " ++ show c ++ " " ++ (show . chr . fromIntegral) c) $
  650 #endif
  651       case fromIntegral c of { IBOX(ord_c) ->
  652         let
  653                 base   = alexIndexInt32OffAddr alex_base s
  654                 offset = PLUS(base,ord_c)
  655 
  656                 new_s = if GTE(offset,ILIT(0))
  657                           && let check  = alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_check offset
  658                              in  EQ(check,ord_c)
  659                           then alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_table offset
  660                           else alexIndexInt16OffAddr alex_deflt s
  661         in
  662         case new_s of
  663             ILIT(-1) -> (new_acc, input__)
  664                 -- on an error, we want to keep the input *before* the
  665                 -- character that failed, not after.
  666             _ -> alex_scan_tkn user__ orig_input
  667 #ifdef ALEX_LATIN1
  668                    PLUS(len,ILIT(1))
  669                    -- issue 119: in the latin1 encoding, *each* byte is one character
  670 #else
  671                    (if c < 0x80 || c >= 0xC0 then PLUS(len,ILIT(1)) else len)
  672                    -- note that the length is increased ONLY if this is the 1st byte in a char encoding)
  673 #endif
  674                    new_input new_s new_acc
  675       }
  676   where
  677         check_accs (AlexAccNone) = last_acc
  678         check_accs (AlexAcc a  ) = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  679         check_accs (AlexAccSkip) = AlexLastSkip  input__ IBOX(len)
  680 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  681         check_accs (AlexAccPred a predx rest)
  682            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  683            = AlexLastAcc a input__ IBOX(len)
  684            | otherwise
  685            = check_accs rest
  686         check_accs (AlexAccSkipPred predx rest)
  687            | predx user__ orig_input IBOX(len) input__
  688            = AlexLastSkip input__ IBOX(len)
  689            | otherwise
  690            = check_accs rest
  691 #endif
  692 
  693 data AlexLastAcc
  694   = AlexNone
  695   | AlexLastAcc !Int !AlexInput !Int
  696   | AlexLastSkip     !AlexInput !Int
  697 
  698 data AlexAcc user
  699   = AlexAccNone
  700   | AlexAcc Int
  701   | AlexAccSkip
  702 #ifndef ALEX_NOPRED
  703   | AlexAccPred Int (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  704   | AlexAccSkipPred (AlexAccPred user) (AlexAcc user)
  705 
  706 type AlexAccPred user = user -> AlexInput -> Int -> AlexInput -> Bool
  707 
  708 -- -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
  709 -- Predicates on a rule
  710 
  711 alexAndPred p1 p2 user__ in1 len in2
  712   = p1 user__ in1 len in2 && p2 user__ in1 len in2
  713 
  714 --alexPrevCharIsPred :: Char -> AlexAccPred _
  715 alexPrevCharIs c _ input__ _ _ = c == alexInputPrevChar input__
  716 
  717 alexPrevCharMatches f _ input__ _ _ = f (alexInputPrevChar input__)
  718 
  719 --alexPrevCharIsOneOfPred :: Array Char Bool -> AlexAccPred _
  720 alexPrevCharIsOneOf arr _ input__ _ _ = arr Data.Array.! alexInputPrevChar input__
  721 
  722 --alexRightContext :: Int -> AlexAccPred _
  723 alexRightContext IBOX(sc) user__ _ _ input__ =
  724      case alex_scan_tkn user__ input__ ILIT(0) input__ sc AlexNone of
  725           (AlexNone, _) -> False
  726           _ -> True
  727         -- TODO: there's no need to find the longest
  728         -- match when checking the right context, just
  729         -- the first match will do.
  730 #endif
  731 {-# LINE 141 "saw-script/src/SAWScript/Lexer.x" #-}
  732 -- token helpers
  733 
  734 type Action = Pos -> Text -> LexS -> ([Token Pos], LexS)
  735 plain ::                   (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Action
  736 xform :: (Text -> Text) -> (Pos -> Text -> Token Pos)   -> Action
  737 addon :: (Text -> a) -> (Pos -> Text -> a -> Token Pos) -> Action
  738 
  739 addToComment, startComment, endComment :: Action
  740 addToCode, startCode, endCode :: Action
  741 addToString, startString, endString :: Action
  742 addToCType, startCType, endCType :: Action
  743 
  744 plain   tok pos txt = \s -> ([tok pos txt], s)         -- ^ just the contents
  745 xform f tok pos txt = \s -> ([tok pos (f txt)], s)     -- ^ transform contents
  746 addon f tok pos txt = \s -> ([tok pos txt (f txt)], s) -- ^ also variant contents
  747 
  748 startComment p txt s = ([], InComment p stack chunks done)
  749   where (stack,chunks, done) = case s of
  750           Normal                 -> ([], [txt], Normal)
  751           InComment q qs cs done -> (q : qs, txt : cs, done)
  752           InCode q ctxt          -> ([], [txt], InCode q ctxt)
  753           InCType q ctxt         -> ([], [txt], InCType q ctxt)
  754           _                      -> panic "[Lexer] startComment" ["not in normal or cryptol block or comment"]
  755 
  756 endComment p txt s =
  757   case s of
  758     InComment f [] cs done     -> ([], addWhitespace f (Text.concat (reverse cs) <> txt) done)
  759     InComment _ (q:qs) cs done -> ([], InComment q qs (txt : cs) done)
  760     _                          -> panic "[Lexer] endComment" ["outside comment"]
  761 
  762 addToComment _ txt s = ([], InComment p stack (txt : chunks) done)
  763   where
  764   (p, stack, chunks, done) =
  765      case s of
  766        InComment q qs cs done -> (q,qs,cs,done)
  767        _                   -> panic "[Lexer] addToComment" ["outside comment"]
  768 
  769 startLineComment p txt s = ([], InLineComment p txt s)
  770 
  771 endLineComment p txt s =
  772   case s of
  773     InLineComment f cs done -> ([], addWhitespace p (cs <> txt) done)
  774     _                    -> panic "[Lexer] endLineComment" ["outside line comment"]
  775 
  776 -- Cryptol is indentation-sensitive. Just deleting the comments could produce
  777 -- unparsable Cryptol , so we replace the removed comments with matching
  778 -- whitespace
  779 addWhitespace p txt s@(InCode q x) = snd $ addToCode p (whiteout txt) s
  780 addWhitespace p txt s@(InCType q x) = snd $ addToCType p (whiteout txt) s
  781 addWhitespace _ _ s = s
  782 
  783 whiteout = Text.map (\c -> if c == '\n' then '\n' else ' ')
  784 
  785 startString p txt s = ([],InString p txt s)
  786 
  787 endString pe txt s = case s of
  788   InString ps str done -> ([mkToken ps str], done)
  789   _               -> panic "[Lexer] endString" ["outside string"]
  790   where
  791   mkToken ps str = TLit (spanPos ps pe) (read' $ str `Text.append` txt)
  792 
  793 addToString _ txt s = case s of
  794   InString p str done -> ([],InString p (str `Text.append` txt) done)
  795   _              -> panic "[Lexer] addToString" ["outside string"]
  796 
  797 startCode p _ _ = ([],InCode p Text.empty)
  798 
  799 endCode pe _ s = case s of
  800   InCode ps str -> ([TCode (spanPos ps pe) str], Normal)
  801   _               -> panic "[Lexer] endCode" ["outside code"]
  802 
  803 addToCode _ txt s = case s of
  804   InCode p str -> ([],InCode p (str `Text.append` txt))
  805   _              -> panic "[Lexer] addToCode" ["outside code"]
  806 
  807 startCType p _ _ = ([],InCType p Text.empty)
  808 
  809 endCType pe _ s = case s of
  810   InCType ps str -> ([TCType (spanPos ps pe) str], Normal)
  811   _               -> panic "[Lexer] endCType" ["outside ctype"]
  812 
  813 addToCType _ txt s = case s of
  814   InCType p str -> ([],InCType p (str `Text.append` txt))
  815   _              -> panic "[Lexer] addToCType" ["outside ctype"]
  816 
  817 -- fetch a value via Read
  818 --
  819 -- XXX: we should not use this for string literals, because as much as
  820 -- it's convenient to have the stdlib decode escape sequences for us,
  821 -- the escape sequences available in SAWScript strings should properly
  822 -- be defined by SAWScript (that is, explicitly here) and not by
  823 -- what's in GHC's standard library.
  824 --
  825 -- FUTURE: it would be nice to get the source position into the panic
  826 -- message in case it ever actually happens, but that seems difficult
  827 -- to arrange.
  828 read' :: Read a => Text -> a
  829 read' txt = case readMaybe txt' of
  830     Just x -> x
  831     Nothing -> panic "Lexer" ["Failed to decode string or number literal", txt]
  832   where txt' = Text.unpack txt
  833 
  834 -- read a binary integer
  835 readBin :: Text -> Integer
  836 readBin s = case readInt 2 isDigit cvt (Text.unpack s') of
  837               [(a, "")] -> a
  838               _         -> panic "Lexer" ["Cannot read a binary number from: ", s]
  839   where cvt c = ord c - ord '0'
  840         isDigit c = c == '0' || c == '1'
  841         s' | "0b" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  842            | "0B" `Text.isPrefixOf` s = Text.drop 2 s
  843            | True                     = s
  844 
  845 
  846 -- alex support and lexer mechanism
  847 
  848 -- current position
  849 data AlexPos = AlexPos {
  850     apLine :: !Int,
  851     apCol :: !Int
  852   }
  853 
  854 -- input state
  855 type AlexInput = (
  856     AlexPos,    -- ^ Current position
  857     Text        -- ^ Remaining input
  858   )
  859 
  860 data LexS
  861   = Normal
  862   | InComment !Pos ![Pos] [Text] LexS
  863   | InLineComment !Pos Text LexS
  864   | InString !Pos Text LexS
  865   | InCode   !Pos Text
  866   | InCType  !Pos Text
  867   deriving (Show)
  868 
  869 stateToInt Normal = 0
  870 stateToInt (InComment {}) = comment
  871 stateToInt (InLineComment {}) = linecomment
  872 stateToInt (InString {}) = string
  873 stateToInt (InCode {}) = code
  874 stateToInt (InCType {}) = ctype
  875 
  876 -- initial position
  877 startPos :: AlexPos
  878 startPos = AlexPos { apLine = 1, apCol = 1 }
  879 
  880 -- feed alex a byte describing the current char
  881 -- this came from Cryptol's lexer, which came from LexerUtils, which
  882 -- adapted the technique used in GHC's lexer.
  883 --
  884 -- FUTURE: it would be nice to share this with the saw-core lexer
  885 -- (and maybe also the Cryptol lexer) instead of pasting it repeatedly
  886 byteForChar :: Char -> Word8
  887 byteForChar c
  888   | c <= '\7' = non_graphic
  889   | Char.isAscii c = fromIntegral (ord c)
  890   | otherwise = case Char.generalCategory c of
  891       Char.LowercaseLetter       -> lower
  892       Char.OtherLetter           -> lower
  893       Char.UppercaseLetter       -> upper
  894       Char.TitlecaseLetter       -> upper
  895       Char.DecimalNumber         -> digit
  896       Char.OtherNumber           -> digit
  897       Char.ConnectorPunctuation  -> symbol
  898       Char.DashPunctuation       -> symbol
  899       Char.OtherPunctuation      -> symbol
  900       Char.MathSymbol            -> symbol
  901       Char.CurrencySymbol        -> symbol
  902       Char.ModifierSymbol        -> symbol
  903       Char.OtherSymbol           -> symbol
  904       Char.Space                 -> sp
  905       Char.ModifierLetter        -> other
  906       Char.NonSpacingMark        -> other
  907       Char.SpacingCombiningMark  -> other
  908       Char.EnclosingMark         -> other
  909       Char.LetterNumber          -> other
  910       Char.OpenPunctuation       -> other
  911       Char.ClosePunctuation      -> other
  912       Char.InitialQuote          -> other
  913       Char.FinalQuote            -> tick
  914       _                          -> non_graphic
  915   where
  916   -- CAUTION: these must match the $uni* values at the top of the file
  917   non_graphic     = 0
  918   upper           = 1
  919   lower           = 2
  920   digit           = 3
  921   symbol          = 4
  922   sp              = 5
  923   other           = 6
  924   tick            = 7
  925 
  926 -- input handler for alex
  927 alexGetByte :: AlexInput -> Maybe (Word8, AlexInput)
  928 alexGetByte (pos, text) = fmap doGet $ Text.uncons text
  929     where
  930       doGet (c, text') = (byteForChar c, (move pos c, text'))
  931       move pos c = case c of
  932           '\n' -> AlexPos { apLine = apLine pos + 1, apCol = 1 }
  933           _ -> pos { apCol = apCol pos + 1 }
  934 
  935 -- the lexer we're generating doesn't use this hook
  936 alexInputPrevChar :: AlexInput -> Char
  937 alexInputPrevChar _ = panic "Lexer" ["alexInputPrevChar"]
  938 
  939 -- read the text of a file, passing in the filename for use in positions
  940 scanTokens :: FilePath -> Text -> ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
  941 scanTokens filename str = go (startPos, str) Normal
  942   where
  943     fillPos pos height width =
  944         let startLine = apLine pos
  945             startCol = apCol pos
  946             endLine = startLine + height
  947             endCol = startCol + width
  948         in
  949         Range filename startLine startCol endLine endCol
  950 
  951     go inp@(pos, str) s = case alexScan inp (stateToInt s) of
  952         AlexEOF -> let pos' = fillPos pos 0 0
  953                        tok = [TEOF pos' "EOF"]
  954                    in case s of
  955             Normal ->
  956                 (tok, Nothing)
  957             InLineComment pos _ _ ->
  958                 (tok, Just (Warn, pos', "Missing newline at end of file"))
  959             InComment pos _ _ _ ->
  960                 (tok, Just (Error, pos, "Unclosed block comment"))
  961             InString pos _ _ ->
  962                 (tok, Just (Error, pos, "Unterminated string"))
  963             InCode pos _ ->
  964                 (tok, Just (Error, pos, "Unclosed cryptol block"))
  965             InCType pos _ ->
  966                 (tok, Just (Error, pos, "Unclosed ctype block"))
  967         AlexError (pos, _) ->
  968             let line' = Text.pack $ show $ apLine pos
  969                 col' = Text.pack $ show $ apCol pos
  970             in
  971             panic "Lexer" [line' <> ":" <> col' <> ": unspecified lexical error"]
  972         AlexSkip inp' len ->
  973             go inp' s
  974         AlexToken inp' len act ->
  975             let text = Text.take len str
  976                 (height, width) = case reverse $ Text.lines text of
  977                     [] -> (0, 0)
  978                     [line] -> (0, Text.length line)
  979                     last : lines -> (length lines, Text.length last)
  980                 pos' = fillPos pos height width
  981             in
  982             let (t, s') = act pos' text s
  983                 (ts, mmsg) = go inp' s'
  984             in (t ++ ts, mmsg)
  985 
  986 -- | Type to hold a diagnostic message (error or warning).
  987 --
  988 -- This should cease to be needed once we clean out the message
  989 -- printing infrastructure. It's here only to shorten the type
  990 -- signatures below, and represents the possibility of having
  991 -- generated a message.
  992 type OptMsg = Maybe (Verbosity, Pos, Text)
  993 
  994 -- entry point
  995 lexSAW :: FilePath -> Text -> ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
  996 lexSAW f text = scanTokens f text
  997 
  998 -- alternate monadic entry point (XXX: does this have any value?)
  999 scan :: Monad m => FilePath -> Text -> m ([Token Pos], OptMsg)
 1000 scan f = return . lexSAW f
